This rudimentary, but revolutionary, bit of equipment, with Bakelite knobs and a collection of rheostat pan-pots, was operated during concerts by Richard Wright. As he operated the joysticks, the source of the sound moved from speaker to speaker around the auditorium. The first model was stolen, but here&#039;s a picture of the replacement:" width="168" height="112" /></div></a><a href="/pinkfloyd/photos/pb.5660597307.-2207520000.1423525649./10152637951807308/?type=1" rel="theater" ajaxify="/pinkfloyd/photos/pb.5660597307.-2207520000.1423525649./10152637951807308/?type=1&amp;src=https%3A%2F%2Ffbcdn-sphotos-h-a.akamaihd.net%2Fhphotos-ak-xfp1%2Fv%2Ft1.0-9%2F10502084_10152637951807308_8340826464151183926_n.jpg%3Foh%3D5065f401809936b44abd03fc8f61b7bf%26oe%3D55947E75%26__gda__%3D1435770896_96bc7e2fe5a7318b8921b00e3c4bfb9b&amp;size=620%2C400&amp;fbid=10152637951807308&amp;source=29&amp;player_origin=pages"><div class="uiScaledImageContainer _5v4k" style="width:111px;height:111px;"><img class="scaledImageFitHeight img" src="https://fbcdn-sphotos-h-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xfp1/v/t1.0-9/s173x172/10502084_10152637951807308_8340826464151183926_n.jpg?oh=3a98dfffde56d536f1193b97d86e2b6b&amp;oe=554A5270&amp;__gda__=1432739465_9324aadc43e5b5c40d7eb48cedf24104" style="left:-31px;" alt="Today in 1988, the Houses of Parliament were overshadowed by the serene sight of a large inflatable bed -
